81:["$","p",null,{"children":"REPL Bridge 的消息流转如下图所示："}]
b0:T45d,sequenceDiagram
    participant User as 用户 (终端/Web)
    participant REPL as REPL 循环
    participant Bridge as replBridge
    participant Transport as WebSocket/SSE
    participant Server as Session Ingress

    Note over User,Server: 出站路径：REPL → Web UI
    REPL->>Bridge: writeMessages(messages)
    Bridge->>Bridge: 过滤 isEligibleBridgeMessage
    Bridge->>Bridge: 转换 toSDKMessages
    Bridge->>Bridge: 过滤 previouslyFlushedUUIDs
    Bridge->>Transport: transport.write(sdkMsg)
    Transport->>Server: WebSocket/SSE POST

    Note over User,Server: 入站路径：Web UI → REPL
    Server->>Transport: WebSocket 消息
    Transport->>Bridge: handleIngressMessage
    Bridge->>Bridge: 回声过滤 (BoundedUUIDSet)
    Bridge->>Bridge: 类型检查 + 路由
    Bridge->>REPL: onInboundMessage(sdkMsg)
    REPL->>REPL: 执行用户请求

    Note over User,Server: 控制路径
    Server->>Transport: control_request (interrupt/set_model)
    Transport->>Bridge: handleServerControlRequest
    Bridge->>REPL: onInterrupt() / onSetModel()
    Bridge->>Transport: control_response82:["$","$L16",null,{"chart":"$b0"}]
